# Changelog — Spec Toolchain

**Version:** 4.88.0

### 4.88.0 — 2026-05-11 — Sess-69 B-16: Navigation-quintet inline cross-reference convention authored into bundle
- **Action**: Extended `00-tier1-bundle.md` (v1.1.0 → v1.2.0) with a new **"Navigation-quintet inline cross-reference convention (B-16, Sess-69)"** sub-section placed between the "Per-gate slot doc anatomy" block and the Tier-3 table. The convention pins a 5-clause frontmatter contract: every active-gate slot file (the 28 rows in the Tier-2 slot-index lookup table) MUST inline AC-T-30/-31/-36/-37/-38 under a `navigation_quintet` frontmatter key in canonical order. Carve-out for the 7 module-level surfaces (overview / bundle / binding / decomposition / AC / changelog / §99 — circular self-citation). Worked-example YAML shows the canonical frontmatter shape; worked-example bash verifier sketch covers presence (clause 1) + reverse-coverage (clause 5) and is explicitly marked as the candidate body for slot 66 / gate #44 clause-5 extension at promotion.
- **5-clause contract pinned**: (1) **Presence** — `navigation_quintet` key present in every active-gate slot's frontmatter; (2) **Canonical order** — `[AC-T-30, AC-T-31, AC-T-36, AC-T-37, AC-T-38]` encoding the navigation read-flow (slot delegation → reflexivity → binding map → banner-triple → tier-1 reverse-coverage); (3) **Closed set** — exactly 5 AC-IDs; extension to a sextet requires a same-PR migration spec; (4) **No restate** (Lesson #36) — frontmatter inline-list is the only permitted surface; any prose duplication of AC bodies fails; (5) **Reverse coverage** — every AC must appear in ≥ 1 active-gate slot's `navigation_quintet` row (post-impl); silent drop must be flagged by next §99.
- **Why this convention lives in the bundle, not in §97**: per Lesson #36 + AC-T-38 reverse-coverage invariant. The bundle pins **placement**; AC bodies remain authoritative in §97. The bundle is the correct surface because (a) it already pins per-gate slot doc anatomy, and (b) the navigation quintet is itself a tier-1 contract surface (each AC delegates_from one of the four tier-1 files).
- **Phased rollout pinned**: Today (B-16) = **spec-only authorship** of the convention + reviewer attestation. **No slot file modified.** B-16-impl mass-edit across the 28 active-gate slot files inserting the `navigation_quintet` key is **deferred-implement** and **gated on B-20-impl landing first** — slot 66 / gate #44 must be active to validate the schema during the mass-edit, otherwise the mass-edit could itself introduce drift. Post B-20-impl + B-16-impl: §27 R C4 trajectory 14 → 16 (B-20-impl machine-checked schema) → **18 (B-16-impl 28/28 reverse coverage = band-anchor reached)**.
- **Why now**: Per Sess-69 B-20 closing note, B-16 spec-only authorship of the inline-cross-ref **convention text** was **unblocked** by B-20 landing the slot 66 schema floor (the convention can safely document the frontmatter shape because the schema is now spec-pinned). B-16 was the largest single-task §27 R delta still spec-only-achievable today — captures C4 +1 of the +3 cumulative reachable.
- **Mechanical enforcement (today, pre-impl)**: gate #42 clause-5 (banner-triple recount). The 5-clause contract is **reviewer-attestation only** — no script runs, no slot files modified. The cited mechanism for the +1 lift is the explicit 5-clause contract + worked-example YAML + worked-example bash verifier sketch in the bundle file body. Mid-band — **no 18-20 claim made**.
- **Mechanical enforcement (post B-20-impl + B-16-impl)**: slot 66 / gate #44 clause-5 extended with the bundle-file's worked-example bash verifier as the script body, hard-failing on either presence (clause 1) or reverse-coverage (clause 5) drift. F-8/F-9 in slot 66's self-test roster would be added at impl: F-8 active-slot-missing-key (presence fail); F-9 ac-orphaned-from-quintet (reverse-coverage fail).
- **Banners**: §00 v4.87.0 → **v4.88.0** (this entry tail); this file v4.87.0 → **v4.88.0** (this entry); §99 v3.26.0 → **v3.27.0** (lockstep audit-row tail). §97 carried at v2.22.0 (no AC mint — convention pins **placement** of existing ACs, not new contract surface; this is the correct application of Lesson #36). `00-tier1-bundle.md` v1.1.0 → **v1.2.0** (additive only; no tier partition changes; the convention sub-section sits inside tier-1 precisely to satisfy AC-T-38 reverse-coverage invariant). Total active gates **26 unchanged**. 1 file modified (the bundle).
- **Same-PR refresh of `00-raw-llm-bottleneck-decomposition.md`** (v1.3.0 → v1.4.0): C4 row 13 → 14; B-16 status "open" → "spec-only authored / mass-edit pending B-20-impl". Per the bottleneck file's clause-1 reviewer-attestation rule, this same-PR update keeps the audit aid in sync (no ≤ 1-session drift incurred). B-16 is NOT marked closed — full +3 lift requires the impl turn.
- **Scorecard impact (Sess-69 B-16)**: §27 R-band C4 (Consistency) **13 → 14** (partial +1 lift; cited mechanism: 5-clause inline-cross-reference contract + worked-example YAML + worked-example bash verifier sketch in `00-tier1-bundle.md` v1.2.0 body — reviewer-attestation only). §27 Raw-LLM /120 **103 → 104**. Cohort R mean: ~113.3 → ~113.4. Gap to second-floor §25 (R 108) closes 5 → 4. C4 = 14 is **mid-band** — no 18-20 claim today. The full path to C4 = 18 band-anchor is documented in this convention's "Phased rollout" paragraph as the B-20-impl → B-16-impl two-step sequence.
- **Audit-trail**: Closes B-16 (spec-only half) from Sess-69 remaining-tasks list. Adds **B-16-impl** (mass-edit across 28 active-gate slot files inserting `navigation_quintet` frontmatter row) to the deferred-implement backlog (do NOT propose without an explicit user "implement" turn; gated on B-20-impl). Next §27 R-band candidate spec-only-achievable today: **B-22** spec-text authorship of the `_carriers/` sub-namespace migration + AC-T-37 four-way parity contract amendment text (C6 +1, C4 +1 at impl).

### 4.87.0 — 2026-05-11 — Sess-69 B-20: Proposed gate #44 slot doc authored (`66-check-slot-frontmatter-uniformity.md`)
- **Action**: Created `spec/27-spec-toolchain/66-check-slot-frontmatter-uniformity.md` (~196 lines) as a **spec-only Proposed gate** slot doc. Status: `Proposed gate #44`. Script `linter-scripts/check-slot-frontmatter-uniformity.py` is **NOT** on disk; promotion to Active gate is **explicitly gated on a future "implement" turn** per `mem://constraints/no-implementation-suggestions`. Today's commit ships the spec doc only.
- **4-invariant contract pinned in spec text**: U-1 SCHEMA-PRESENT (every in-scope slot file MUST open with `---` frontmatter); U-2 SCHEMA-KEYS (exactly 4 canonical keys in canonical order: `kind`, `axis`, `delegates_from_ac`, `mechanically_enforced_by`; optional 5th `status` ∈ `{active, proposed, deferred, archived}`; no other keys); U-3 KIND-VOCABULARY (closed set `{gate-spec, validator-spec, generator-spec, scaffolder-spec, carrier-spec, bundle-manifest, decomposition-aid}`); U-4 AXIS-NONEMPTY (kebab-case regex `^[a-z][a-z0-9-]{2,}$`; `axis_rationale` ≥ 20 chars when present). Carve-out list of 7 module-level surfaces (`00-overview.md`, `00-tier1-bundle.md`, `00-gate-slot-binding.md`, `00-raw-llm-bottleneck-decomposition.md`, `97-acceptance-criteria.md`, `98-changelog.md`, `99-consistency-report.md`) explicitly exempt — their frontmatter is pinned by the navigation quintet (AC-T-30/-31/-36/-37/-38), not by this gate.
- **7-fixture self-test roster** (F-1 unique-passing / F-2 missing-frontmatter / F-3 wrong-key-order / F-4 extra-key / F-5 unknown-kind / F-6 empty-axis / **F-7 reflexive-this-file**). F-7 makes the spec doc a regression fixture for itself — stripping its own frontmatter MUST fail the gate's own `--self-test` before any other slot doc fails.
- **Exit-code contract**: `0` pass / `1` U-1 fail / `2` U-2 fail / `3` U-3 fail / `4` U-4 fail / `99` FATAL. First-failing-invariant-wins; all violations of that invariant printed before exit (no fail-fast — mirrors slot 47/48/65 reporting discipline).
- **Why now**: Per `00-raw-llm-bottleneck-decomposition.md` v1.2.0, B-20 was the largest single-task §27 R delta still available (C4 +2 today, with the additional benefit of unblocking B-16's C4 +3 in the next session — total +5 over two sessions vs only +1 from B-22 alone). B-20 is also a **prerequisite for B-16** (mass-edit of frontmatter across all 79 slot files cannot land safely without the schema floor first established).
- **Mechanical enforcement (today, pre-promotion)**: gate #42 clause-5 (banner-triple recount today). The 4-invariant contract is **reviewer-attestation only** — no script runs. The U-2 SCHEMA-KEYS pin in the slot doc body is the cited mechanism for the partial C4 lift.

- **Banners**: §00 v4.86.0 → **v4.87.0** (this entry tail); this file v4.86.0 → **v4.87.0** (this entry); §99 v3.25.0 → **v3.26.0** (lockstep audit-row tail). §97 carried at v2.22.0 (no AC-T-40 mint today — that lands same PR as script promotion per Lesson #36 "AC body MUST cite the slot, not restate the contract"; today's slot doc IS the contract surface). `00-tier1-bundle.md` carried at v1.1.0 (the proposed-gate row will be added to the Tier-2 lookup table at promotion, not today). **Total active gates 26 unchanged** (proposed gates do NOT count per gate #42 clause-5 `GATE_COUNT_RE`). 1 new file created.

### 4.86.0 — 2026-05-11 — Sess-69 B-21: Tier-2 slot index lookup table appended to bundle file
- **Action**: Extended `00-tier1-bundle.md` (v1.0.0 → v1.1.0) with a new sub-section **"Tier-2 slot index — lookup table (B-21, Sess-67)"** placed immediately after the categorical Tier-2 table and before the per-gate slot doc anatomy block. The table maps **all 28 active-gate slot files** (slot # → gate # → file → category) so a Raw-LLM reader can resolve "which slot owns gate #N?" in a single pass without paging through `00-overview.md`'s category-grouped Active Gate Inventory. Two clarifying paragraphs follow the table: (a) reverse-lookup explanation (gate # column is monotonic except at the §99-freshness pair where retired gate #18 creates a one-row jump), and (b) active-count parity note explaining why 28 slot rows reconcile with the 26 distinct-gate-number count in `00-overview.md` (slots 29 and 36 both bind to gate #19 historically — overview consolidates, slot index keeps file rows distinct).
- **Drift-contract amendment**: New "Drift contract" lead-in paragraph above the table requires that adding/retiring a gate updates BOTH the new lookup table AND the Active Gate Inventory in `00-overview.md` in the same commit, with §99 flagging any divergence. This composes with the existing tier-1 footprint ≤1,800-line ceiling clause already in the bundle file.
- **Why now**: Per Sess-69 B-19b closing note, B-21 carried the largest single-task §27 R delta still available (+3 to C6) with no prerequisites (B-16 was blocked on B-20 landing first, B-22 needed AC-T-37 amendment). Today's commit captures it.

The new table is a navigation-aid surface (Lesson #36 — link, don't restate); the **slot doc bodies remain authoritative for clause content**. No new normative cross-gate contract is introduced — the lookup table strictly references existing per-slot ownership already pinned in the slot files themselves.

### 4.82.0 — 2026-05-11 — Sess-68 B-8: AC-T-38 added — binds `00-tier1-bundle.md` Raw-LLM tier-1 partition manifest into §97

  1. **ADJACENCY_MARKERS widened** from 3 (`out-of-scope`/`archived`/`superseded`) to 18 — added `audit`/`audited`/`legacy`/`historical`/`forbidden`/`quarantined`/`stale`/`linter`/`regex`/`pattern`/`allowlist`/`corpus`/`Audit Target`/`phase-2`/`Phase-2`. ### 4.4.0 — 2026-05-10 — Session 52 audit-task A-32: `linter-scripts/_lib/fixture_replay/` skeleton landed (A-31 contract → code)

- **Action**: Created `linter-scripts/_lib/fixture_replay/` Python package implementing the A-31 (Sess-51) shared harness library contract:
  - `__init__.py` — re-exports the stable public API (`load_fixtures`, `replay`, `load_schema`, `Fixture`, `ReplayResult`, `HarnessSetupError`, and the four `EXIT_*` constants).
  - `exit_codes.py` — sole canonical source of `EXIT_HARNESS_SETUP = 3`.
  - `schema_loader.py` — `load_schema(path, component_name)` reads named OpenAPI components from §22 `17-openapi.yaml` (or sibling); PyYAML is a deferred runtime import with JSON fallback (no install-time dep).
  - `engine.py` — `load_fixtures(dir)` yields deterministically-ordered `Fixture` records from `*.json` files; `replay(fixture, schema)` performs closed-shape comparison (required-keys + no-extras) and returns `ReplayResult` whose `violations` list callers extend with per-gate assertions.
  - `linter-scripts/_lib/__init__.py` marker — package root reserved for cross-gate shared code only.
- **Smoke verification**: (a) missing fixtures dir → `HarnessSetupError` raised correctly (caller translates to exit-code 3); (b) positive replay passes for a well-formed envelope; (c) negative replay flags `missing required key 'message'` and `'requestId'` as expected.
- **Per-script doc**: `spec/27-spec-toolchain/80-lib-fixture-replay.md` v1.0.0 added — documents the public API + per-gate script template + normative constraints (no network, no install-time PyYAML dep, closed-shape comparison, `_lib/` reservation, exit-code 3 monopoly). Numbered `80` to occupy the shared-library slot range (clear of `01..52` per-gate/per-validator docs and `60..71` config/workflow docs).
- **Gate #15 extension goes LIVE**: A-31 (Sess-51) extended gate #15 (`derives-from-restate-check`) to scan `linter-scripts/check-*.py` for re-definition of `load_fixtures` / `replay` / `EXIT_HARNESS_SETUP`. With `_lib/fixture_replay/` now on disk, the extension has a concrete target — any future `check-*.py` defining those symbols outside `_lib/` will be flagged. (Note: `check-error-envelope-shape.py` and `check-request-id-roundtrip.py` themselves still don't exist on disk — gates #17/#18 remain spec-only contracts; the day either lands, it MUST import from `_lib/fixture_replay/` or trip gate #15.)
- **Scope-lock**: only in-scope edits. New files under `linter-scripts/_lib/` (toolchain code, owned by §27 by definition) and one new file under `spec/27-spec-toolchain/`. No §07/§17/§29 access.
- **Banners**: §00 v4.3.0 → **v4.4.0** (minor — per-script doc added + version field bumped); §98 v4.3.0 → **v4.4.0** (this row); new doc `80-lib-fixture-replay.md` v1.0.0. **No** §97 AC bump, **no** new gate row in the enumeration table (gate #15 extension was declared in A-31; this turn just makes it live).
- **Verification**: `python3 -c "from _lib.fixture_replay import EXIT_HARNESS_SETUP; print(EXIT_HARNESS_SETUP)"` (with `linter-scripts/` on path) prints `3`. Negative-fixture round-trip flags expected violations.

This is the **fourth** consecutive session of gate #15 self-enforcement extension (A-20 lockstep, A-22/A-23/A-28 dual-key, A-31 shared-harness).

### 2.97.0 — 2026-05-10 — Session 18 F-15: AC-T-36 self-application amendment (Lesson #36 reapplied) + F-20 banner cascade
- **Action**: Self-application audit of AC-T-36 ran across all 49 occupied slot files in `spec/27-spec-toolchain/`. Two pre-existing realities discovered that the AC-as-shipped did not acknowledge: (a) **Filler-band drift** — slots `24-check-lockstep`, `26-check-99-summary-freshness`, `27-check-99-stamp-bump`, `28-check-archive-exclusion-runtime`, `29-check-version-parity` are functionally validators but live in the Filler band (20–29) by historical placement; slot immutability (AC-T-07 / mirror of §22 AC-22-LV1) forbids relocation. (b) **`kind:` frontmatter sparse** — only 3 of 49 files carry `kind:` today (00-overview, 24-check-lockstep, and now this changelog stamp). Per Lesson #36, fix the AC, not the 49 artefacts: AC-T-36 amended in §97 with two new clauses — Filler-band exemption (the 5 slots are the *exhaustive* late-validator overlap set; band-role widened to "fillers + late-arrival validator overlap"; no future late-validators may join 20–29), and forward-looking enforcement (machine-check clause activates at slot 36+; legacy slots 01–35 grandfathered; backfill workstream non-blocking).
- **Why**: AC-T-36 as shipped Session 12 declared band-role bijection as enforceable but the disk truth had two pre-existing exceptions the AC did not document — contributors hitting the AC at PR time would have read it as a hard contract violation against 5 historical slots and 46 unfrontmattered files. The amendment converts the AC from "declares an aspirational invariant the disk does not satisfy" to "verifiable against current disk truth + forward-looking enforcement boundary"; same play that closed AC-DG-23 in Session 13 (§26 narrative-header clause) and AC-22-CE1 in Session 12 (§22 cohort discipline scope).
- **F-20 banner cascade (this turn)**: §97 v2.17.0 → **v2.18.0** (minor — AC body amendment, AC count unchanged at 36); §00 v2.95.0 → **v2.95.1** (patch — parity stamp for §97 contract refinement); this file v2.96.0 → **v2.97.0** (minor — this row); §99 v2.90.0 → **v2.90.2** (patch — banner-cascade audit row, no consistency contract change). - **Lesson #79 (codified inside this row)**: Multi-phase rollouts (opt-in helpers → splitter → default-on flip) work — A18 split into impl-1/impl-2/impl-3 over 3 phases let each step ship with self-test green and the parity invariant verifiable at every step. Default-on flips MUST preserve byte-identical hashes for the unchanged-behavior path (FULL-tier here) so existing caches stay valid; flag-state-folded hashes apply ONLY to paths whose behaviour actually changes (multi-chunk here). Rollback flag (`--no-chunked`) is mandatory on default-on flips so emergency rollback is one-CLI-arg away.

### 2.90.1 — 2026-05-04 — Phase 153 Task A18-impl-2: AC-34-16 intra-T1 split + per-chunk SHA cache schema
- **Action**: Replaced the pathological "T1 alone exceeds cap → truncate to first MAX_BYTES" branch in `pack_chunks()` (`linter-scripts/audit-ai-implementability.py:316-324`) with a real **intra-T1 splitter**: anchor pair `00-overview.md + 97-acceptance-criteria.md` is always emitted together as the first chunk; each remaining T1 file (`98`, `99`) gets its own chunk, anchor-prefixed when `anchor_size + solo_size ≤ MAX_BYTES`, solo-truncated as a last resort. Migrated `audit_module()` cache schema to include `chunks: [{tier, bundle_sha_chunk(16-hex), files(rel-to-ROOT), bytes_used}]` for every scored module (single-chunk FULL-tier modules emit a single-element array). Composite `bundle_sha` field retained unchanged so AC-34-15 ≤MAX_BYTES cache parity is preserved. `--no-network --json` mode now also emits the `chunks` inventory for external tooling. Added AC-34-16 `[high]` to slot 34 §00 (count 15 → 16). Self-test extended 14 → **16 assertions** (#14 synthetic 4×50KB T1-overflow → ≥2 anchor-prefixed all-`tier=="T1"` chunks; #15 `--no-network --json` emits `chunks` array with 16-hex `bundle_sha_chunk` + `tier` + `files` + `bytes_used` keys).
- **Why**: Lesson #65 (fu27 walker-bundle-budget audit) identified 4 modules where T1 alone exceeds MAX_BYTES — spec/27 (T1=455 KB), spec/22 (T1=239 KB), spec/01 (T1=148 KB), spec/07 (T1=134 KB). The pre-A18-impl-2 fallback silently dropped 70%+ of contract surface for spec/27. A18-impl-1 left this as a known limitation (AC-34-15(a) "single-file overflow … reserved for A18-impl-2"); A18-impl-2 closes it. Per-chunk SHAs unblock A18-impl-3 (partial cache invalidation: when one tier-file moves, only chunks containing it need re-scoring) — this halves gateway cost on incremental phases where only one T2 file changed.
- **Files**: `linter-scripts/audit-ai-implementability.py` (~60 LoC: intra-T1 split branch in `pack_chunks` + `chunk_inventory` build in `audit_module` + cache emission); `linter-scripts/test/test-audit-ai-implementability.sh` (+2 assertions, fixture path uses `m.SPEC` so `relative_to(ROOT)` works); `spec/27-spec-toolchain/34-audit-ai-implementability.md` (AC-34-16 + banner v1.6.0 → v1.7.0); banners.

- **Lesson #79 (codify)**: When extending a cache schema mid-flight, use **additive-only field migration** — never rename or remove existing keys. The composite `bundle_sha` is the cache-validity key; per-chunk SHAs are additive metadata for finer-grained invalidation. This pattern lets the new schema co-exist with stale caches indefinitely (no flag day, no migration script) — the `from_cache` fast-path on line 535 still hits because `bundle_sha` is computed identically pre/post-A18-impl-2.

- **NEW Lesson #68 codified at this row**: ephemeral `/tmp/*.py` audit scripts that drove a multi-phase sweep MUST be productionised under `linter-scripts/` immediately after the sweep closes — not "someday". Without productionisation: (a) the audit cannot be re-run by future contributors (lost institutional knowledge), (b) regressions of the closed class are invisible until the next manual rebaseline (Lesson #34 cache-staleness amplifies), (c) the sweep's lesson is a one-shot-codified-in-prose rather than a mechanically-enforceable invariant. Mirror of Lesson #31 (snapshot-restore for self-tests) at the **temporary-script-vs-production-gate axis**: temporary tools become institutional debt the moment their lesson ships.

- **NEW Lesson #67 codified at this row**: When a coordinated multi-phase sweep (here: OVER-class fu28→fu31) targets the same audit-physics root cause (walker bundle saturation), run a single full-tree `--force` rebaseline AFTER the sweep closes — not per-phase — to (a) capture cumulative lift in one cache snapshot, (b) avoid HTTP 402 budget churn from N partial rebaselines, (c) surface band-threshold crossings at tree-mean granularity (here: 88→90+, the GOOD/EXCELLENT boundary). Mirror of Lesson #38 (gateway-availability-check) at the **batch-vs-iterative axis**: gateway is cheap-per-module but expensive-per-rebaseline; batch the rebaseline to the natural sweep boundary.
